阿洁塔舰桥问答

返回舰桥问答目录

Sororitas

条件选项

  • 显示条件：Etude；“再和我说一下，我们被带走之后，你遇到了什么事情？”
  • 显示条件：Etude；“我们得想办法逃出这个地方。”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“你之前说，你有个私人请求，是吗？”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected、Quest；“你准备好陪我进入授状大厅了吗？”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“我还在等着你和我讲讲你的过去。落脚港那个邪教徒说的怪话是什么意思？和我解释一下吧。”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“你觉得我该送给婕伊什么样的礼物？”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“每位修女都真的像你说得那样毫无瑕疵吗？”
  • 检定：SkillLoreImperium / Easy / DC 55；“普罗图斯修会并不是武装修会，但你依然是位训练有素的战士。”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“普罗图斯修会并不是武装修会，但你依然是位训练有素的战士。”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected、Quest；“你刚刚说，你的修会属于卡利西斯分支，那你为什么会来科罗努斯扩区？”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“和我说说你自己的事情吧。”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“你是怎么上了西奥多拉的船？”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected；“我们可以去那颗行星，收拾那些崇拜混沌的异端分子。”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“你准备好告诉我更多你自己的事情了吗？”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“你随身带着的那个金色碎片……”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected；“我想进一步了解你的事情。”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“我想讨论一下萨利斯主星，以及你在寻找的圣物。”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected；“这个故事里的女孩就是圣阿洁塔吗？”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“是什么原因让你一直留在我身边？”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“我希望你能离开我的船，离开我随行人员的行列。”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“我想跟你讨论一下，你从欧夫拉茨二号星的战斗中了解到了什么事情？”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“你的朝圣之旅已经结束了，你还愿意继续跟随我吗？”

问答正文

“行商浪人！能与帝皇的神选者重聚，这让我的灵魂无比慰藉！”
"Rogue Trader! Being reunited with the Emperor's chosen is a balm to my soul!"

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice

“再和我说一下，我们被带走之后，你遇到了什么事情？”
"Remind me: what happened to you after we were taken?"

  • 选择 Choice

“你有没有想办法了解到这个地方的情况？”
"Have you managed to learn anything about this place?"

“我根本没打算过要这么做！我有什么必要了解人类之敌的堕落之举？我只想用汹涌而纯净的烈焰将它付之一炬。这个地方充满了邪恶，但帝皇沦落此地的仆人需要拯救。这就是我需要知道的一切，我已经知道了。”
"I have made no attempt to do so! What need do I have to know of the depravity of the enemies of Humanity, when all I want is to burn it all in pure, raging flame? I already know all I need to — this place is evil, but there are servants of the Emperor here worthy of salvation."

  • 选择 Choice

“我们得想办法逃出这个地方。”
"We need to find a way out of here."

“如果我们的盟友是信仰帝皇的同志，而不是令人厌恶的怪物，我们本可以找到出路！可现在，政委已经死了，我们只能靠我们自己了。”
"We would find a way out if we joined forces with a comrade in faith, and not a repulsive monster! But now the Commissar is dead, and we are on our own."

“我们会的。我发誓要为了这个目标而战，绝不会失去希望，即使……即使我们已经被欺骗、腐化与背叛团团包围！”
"We do. And I swear to fight for that end and not to lose hope, even... even when deceit, corruption, and treachery surround us on all sides!"

  • 选择 Choice

“我得告辞了。”
"I must take my leave."

“愿泰拉之光与你同在，行商浪人！”
"May Terra's light be with you, Rogue Trader!"

阿洁塔热忱地低声祈祷着，呼唤神圣的烈焰净化你们所处的黑暗之地。
Argenta fervently whispers a prayer, calling down holy flame to cleanse this dark place in which you find yourselves.

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice

“再和我说一下，我们被带走之后，你遇到了什么事情？”
"Remind me: what happened to you after we were taken?"

  • 选择 Choice

“你有没有想办法了解到这个地方的情况？”
"Have you managed to learn anything about this place?"

“我根本没打算过要这么做！我有什么必要了解人类之敌的堕落之举？我只想用汹涌而纯净的烈焰将它付之一炬。这个地方充满了邪恶，但帝皇沦落此地的仆人需要拯救。这就是我需要知道的一切，我已经知道了。”
"I have made no attempt to do so! What need do I have to know of the depravity of the enemies of Humanity, when all I want is to burn it all in pure, raging flame? I already know all I need to — this place is evil, but there are servants of the Emperor here worthy of salvation."

  • 选择 Choice

“我们得想办法逃出这个地方。”
"We need to find a way out of here."

“如果我们的盟友是信仰帝皇的同志，而不是令人厌恶的怪物，我们本可以找到出路！可现在，政委已经死了，我们只能靠我们自己了。”
"We would find a way out if we joined forces with a comrade in faith, and not a repulsive monster! But now the Commissar is dead, and we are on our own."

“我们会的。我发誓要为了这个目标而战，绝不会失去希望，即使……即使我们已经被欺骗、腐化与背叛团团包围！”
"We do. And I swear to fight for that end and not to lose hope, even... even when deceit, corruption, and treachery surround us on all sides!"

  • 选择 Choice

“我得告辞了。”
"I must take my leave."

“愿泰拉之光与你同在，行商浪人！”
"May Terra's light be with you, Rogue Trader!"

阿洁塔修女看起来很疲惫。她的眼睛下面带着黑眼圈，头发有些凌乱，动作看起来也有些紧绷“行商浪人？”
Sister Argenta looks tired — there are dark circles under her eyes, her hair is somewhat dishevelled, and she moves like she's a little on edge. "Rogue Trader?"

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice

“你之前说，你有个私人请求，是吗？”
"You said you have a personal request for me?"

“我确实有个请求，行商浪人。”
"I indeed have a request, Rogue Trader."

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice
  • 选择 Choice
  • 选择 Choice
  • 选择 Choice
  • 选择 Choice
  • 选择 Choice

“你准备好陪我进入授状大厅了吗？”
"Are you ready to accompany me to the Warrant Chamber?"

阿洁塔感激地点点头。
Argenta nods gratefully.

  • 选择 Choice

“我还在等着你和我讲讲你的过去。落脚港那个邪教徒说的怪话是什么意思？和我解释一下吧。”
"I'm waiting for you to tell me about your past and to explain the strange words of that cultist on Footfall."

“是的，我已经准备好了！我只请求一件事情，行商浪人。如果可以的话，我希望能看看保存神圣授状的房间，跪在由帝皇本人触碰过的圣物前。这会是一场艰难的对话……我希望在将我的灵魂表露无遗之前，能先在圣物旁边祈祷。”
"Yes. I'm ready! I would ask only one thing of you, Rogue Trader. If I may, I would like to see the chamber of the sacred Warrant and kneel before the relic touched by the Emperor Himself. A difficult conversation lies ahead of us... and I wish to pray by the relic before I lay my soul bare."

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice

“没问题，我们立刻过去吧。”
"Of course. Let us go there right away."

阿洁塔感激地点点头。
Argenta nods gratefully.

  • 选择 Choice

“现在还不行。”
"Not now."

“好吧……行商浪人。我会保持耐心，静静等待。”
"Well... then I will be patient, Rogue Trader, and wait."

  • 选择 Choice

“你觉得我该送给婕伊什么样的礼物？”
"What kind of gift do you think I could give Jae?"

“如果你真的想为她好，就送她一些良知和对帝皇的敬畏吧！这才是她真正需要的东西。但如果你只是想取悦她的话……就送她一些昂贵闪亮，但毫无意义的珠宝吧。这种小玩意对她这样的人，有着神奇般的魔力。”
"If you want to do her good, give her a dose of conscience and fear of the Emperor — that is what she truly needs. But if you want to please her... give her some meaningless jewellery, expensive and shiny. Such baubles wield magical power over hearts like hers."

  • 选择 Choice

“和我说说修女会的情况吧。”
"Tell me about the Adepta Sororitas."

“我很乐意。没有人比我的姐妹更加忠于神皇。我们遵循着神圣国教的意志，与祂的敌人作战，我们……”阿洁塔住了口，哼了一声。“请原谅，行商浪人。看看我啊，我说的这些话，就连帝国的小贵族都早已了如指掌！你具体想了解哪些方面呢？”
"Gladly. There are none more faithful to the God-Emperor than my sisters. We fight against His enemies by the will of the holy Ecclesiarchy, we..." Argenta interrupts herself and snorts. "I beg your pardon, Rogue Trader. Here I am, talking about what every lesser noble in the Imperium knows! So what exactly are you interested in hearing about?"

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice

“人们都说，修女会的修女是整个帝国之中最虔诚的战士。这是真的吗？”
"They say the Adepta Sororitas are the fiercest in their faith among the warriors of the Imperium. Is it true?"

“是这样的！战斗修女是神皇亲手点燃的烈焰。我们是祂的话语的回声，在黑暗的宇宙中四处散播。我们会将祂的愤怒带给异端分子、变种人，以及其他一切人类之敌。我们会保护虔诚之人免受邪恶与亵渎的伤害。有的时候是用祈祷，而更多的时候，是用爆矢枪。”
"It is! The Sisters of Battle are a fire lit by the God-Emperor. They are the echo of His voice that travels through the dark expanses of the universe. We bring His wrath to heretics, mutants, and other enemies of Humanity. We protect the faithful from the unholy and unhallowed. Sometimes with words. More often than not, with a bolter."

  • 选择 Choice

“每位修女都真的像你说得那样毫无瑕疵吗？”
"Are all sisters truly as faultless as you say?"

“即便是修女会的新兵，也都是从最优秀的那些人中挑选出来的。至于那些许下誓言，成为修女会正式成员的人，她们都是精英中的精英，都通过了肉体与精神的双重考验。没错，确实有少数修女表现出了软弱态度，或是踏上了歧途，但别以为我会犯下这样的堕落与罪行。”
"Even the novices of the Adepta Sororitas are drawn from among the most worthy. Those who have taken the vows and become a full-fledged sister are the best of the best, tested by trials of body and spirit. Yes, there have been cases when a sister stumbled or showed weakness. But do not expect to hear a story of depravity or downfall from me."

“每当发生这样的事情，对我们所有人而言都是个巨大的悲剧。哪怕是最微小的黑暗，也不该在光明内部出现！因此，但凡是犯了错，或是表现出软弱态度的人，都会得到赎罪的机会。那些人被称为‘忏悔修女’。敌人会在她们面前颤抖，因为她们渴望战胜弱点、净化罪恶，没有任何事情能阻止这样的战斗修女。”
"Each such occurrence is a great tragedy for us all. Light cannot bear the smallest speck of darkness within! And thus those who have trespassed or shown weakness of spirit are given a chance at redemption. They are called Sisters Repentia, and may the enemy tremble before her, for nothing can stop a Sister of Battle who yearns to be cleansed of faults and weakness."

“她们只穿长袍，不着盔甲，手里拿着开膛剑。那些姐妹曾在信仰的道路上踌躇不前，她们会在战场上找到救赎。尽管她们通常活不了多久，但以赎罪之名而死，总比带着阴影活着要好。”
"Wearing nothing but robes, no armour, Eviscerator in hand, those sisters who have once faltered find repentance on the battlefield. Their lives are seldom long, but a death in the name of purgation is a better fate than to live with a shadow in one's soul."

  • 选择 Choice

“你从属于哪个修会？”
"What order are you from?"

“当我从见习修女的身份毕业之后，我就被派往殉教圣女修会的卡利西斯分部，分配到了普罗图斯修会。普罗图斯修女负责保护帝国的伟大圣物，我们肩负着崇高而重要的使命，负责守卫、保存这些圣物。当这些圣物需要带到战场上，或是需要供朝圣者瞻仰时，我们还会负责护送它们。”
"Once I had completed my novitiate, I was sent to the Calixian branch of the Order of Our Martyred Lady, assigned to the Orders Pronatus. The order's mission is vital and noble — the Sisters Pronatus protect great relics of the Imperium. We guard them, preserve them, escort them when they are brought onto the battlefield or presented for pilgrims to venerate."

“不仅如此，我们还会寻找已经遗失的圣物。一旦普罗图斯修女下定决心，决定将帝国的伟大遗产送回信徒的手中，那无论是异端分子，还是最危险的死亡世界，都无法阻止她们。”
"And we seek out the relics that have been lost. Neither a coven of heretics nor the most wicked death world can deter Sisters Pronatus when their goal is to return a piece of the great legacy of the Imperium into the hands of the faithful."

  • 选择 / Choice（SkillLoreImperium / Easy / DC 55）:

“普罗图斯修会并不是武装修会，但你依然是位训练有素的战士。”
"The Order Pronatus is not one of the Orders Militant. And yet you are a trained fighter."

“别被这个名字骗了。武装修会负责提供军事化训练，让修女们像军队一样踏上战场，但这并不意味着非武装修会的修女脆弱无助。”
"Don't let the name deceive you. The 'Orders Militant' train sisters to march onto the battlefield as an army. That does not make sisters who belong to the non-militant orders timid and helpless."

“无论是带来慰藉的医护修女，还是负责教化的书记修女，都知道该如何对付人类之敌。她们与异端分子之间的‘对话’往往非常简短，而且最后一个字一定会是爆矢枪的炮火！”
"Both the solace-bringing Sisters Hospitaller and the enlightened Sisters Dialogus know how to greet enemies of Humanity. Their 'dialogue' with heretics is usually quite short, with the last word being a bolter discharge!"

阿洁塔顿了顿，声音中带着些许傲慢，急匆匆地补充道。“至于我所在的修会，更是以修女高超的武艺而闻名。我们可是帝国圣物的守护者！如果连普罗图斯修女都无法守护这些圣物，那些受祝福的英雄遗物会变成什么样子？”
After a short pause, Argenta adds with somewhat arrogant haste, "And my order has all the more reason to be known for the martial prowess of its sisters. We are the keepers of the Imperium's relics! What would become of our blessed heroes' legacy if the Sisters Pronatus could not protect it?"

  • 选择 Choice

“你刚刚说，你的修会属于卡利西斯分支，那你为什么会来科罗努斯扩区？”
"You said you belong to the Calixian branch of your order. What brought you to the Koronus Expanse?"

“是修会派我来落脚港的，我的任务是协助当地的德鲁苏斯修会，守护神圣的圣骨匣。这个圣骨匣早在落脚港创始人帕西姆斯·德维恩的时代，就已经放在那里了。”
"The order sent me to Footfall. My undertaking was to assist the local priesthood of Drusians in caring for a sacred reliquary that had been there since the time of Parsimus Dewain, the station's founder."

  • 选择 Choice

“科罗努斯扩区还有修女会的其他成员吗？”
"Are there any other members of the Adepta Sororitas in the Koronus Expanse?"

“据我所知没有，但修女会有很多修会，每个修会都可以独立运作，将她们的修女送到国教认为该去的地方。或许我的姐妹们此刻正在大审判官身边履行她们的职责？愿神皇祝福她们的道路。我希望会是这样，如果能与她们一起祈祷、一起训练，哪怕只有一个晚上的时间，也会令我快乐无比！”
"None that I'm aware of, but the Sisterhood's orders are many and can operate independently of one another, sending their sisters wherever their presence is needed as deemed by the Ecclesiarchy. Perhaps somewhere in the Lord Inquisitor's retinue, may his path be blessed, my sisters perform their duty as we speak? I wish it were so — even a single evening spent in joint prayer and training would bring me joy!"

  • 选择 Choice

“关于修女会，我没有别的问题要问了。”
"I have no more questions about the Sisterhood."

“如果你还有别的问题要问，无须藏在心里，这并不合适！对神圣之物感兴趣是一种美德。”
"Should any more arise — keeping them to yourself would be imprudent! It is a virtue to take an interest in holiness."

  • 选择 Choice

“和我说说你自己的事情吧。”
"Tell me about yourself."

“我自己的事情？”她看起来很惊讶。“我是帝皇的女儿，也是祂的仆人。关于我，还有什么可说的？”
"About me?" She looks surprised. "I am the Emperor's daughter and His servant. What else is there to tell about me?"

  • 选择 Choice

“你是怎么上了西奥多拉的船？”
"How did you end up on Theodora's ship?"

阿洁塔的表情明显变得黯淡下来。“我第一次上她的船，是为了从落脚港前往某颗偏僻的行星。但我猜，你感兴趣的并不是我的第一次旅行，而是在异端分子袭击之前，我出于什么原因上了她的船。这个故事很复杂，我当时只是碰巧……”她突然顿住了。
Argenta's expression darkens visibly. "I first came here when I found myself in need of passage from Footfall to a remote planet. But I imagine what interests you is not that first journey, but rather what brought me aboard prior to the cultist attack. That story is complicated. It just so happened that I..." She stops short.

“我当时犯了个错误。我一时懈怠，遭到了混沌大敌邪恶仆从的伏击。我受了重伤，西奥多拉夫人前来救援。她把我带到了她的船上，让她的船员照顾虚弱不堪的我。这一切就发生在不久之前，因为那些异端分子袭击的时候，我的伤势几乎还没恢复过来。说真的，那些邪恶的仆从简直是一刻不停地筹谋！根本没有任何地方可以免遭他们的阴谋所害。”
"I made a mistake. In a moment of laxity, I was ambushed by the accursed followers of the Archenemy. I was badly wounded. Lady Theodora came to my aid and brought me aboard her ship, where her crew attended to me in my weakened state. It all happened not too long ago — I had barely recovered from my wounds when the cultists struck. Truly the servants of evil know no rest! There is no place where we can be safe from their machinations."

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice

“那些打伤你的人怎么样了？西奥多拉的人消灭他们了吗？”
"What happened to the people who wounded you? Did Theodora's men eliminate them?"

“遗憾的是，那些敌人并没有被消灭。西奥多拉夫人当时很着急，没有继续在那颗行星上停留。当我不省人事的时候，她的人把我带到了船上，而当我醒过来的时候，我们早已飞走了。噢，我真希望能再次面对那些异端分子！总有一天，我会再次面对他们。”
"Sadly, they did not. Lady Theodora was in a hurry and chose not to stay on the planet. Her people took me to her ship while I was unconscious, and when I came to my senses, we were already flying away. Oh, how I pray to come face to face with those heretics once more! And it's bound to happen someday."

  • 选择 Choice

“让你承认犯了错误就这么难吗？”
"Is it difficult for you to accept that you made a mistake?"

“就算是我们之中最出色的人，也难免会犯错误！”阿洁塔激愤地说道，随后她皱起眉头，低下了头。“我的错误是我肩上的重担，我会想办法赎罪的。”
"It happens even to the best of us!" Argenta says heatedly. Then she frowns and lowers her head for a moment. "My mistakes are my burden to bear. I'll find a way to atone for them."

  • 选择 Choice

“这件事情是在什么地方发生的？”
"Where did this happen?"

“是在科罗努斯扩区最近才发现的行星，根本没人想到它早已被异端分子玷污。如果我当时知道这件事情的话，我肯定会提高警惕。”
"On one of the recently discovered planets in the Expanse. No one suspected that it had already been tainted by the filth of heresy. Had I known it beforehand — of course I would have been on my guard."

  • 选择 Choice

“我们可以去那颗行星，收拾那些崇拜混沌的异端分子。”
"We could go to that planet and deal with the Chaos worshippers."

阿洁塔的眼睛亮了起来。她犹豫了一会儿，随后叹息着摇了摇头。“通往那颗行星的航道已经找不到了。随着前任导航者的离世，我们所有的知识都遗落了。想要重新找到这条航道，恐怕要耗费大量人力与资源。冯·瓦兰修斯王朝的继承人肯定有很多别的问题急需处理。或许过些日子……等到我们头上的天空放晴之后再说也不迟。”
Argenta's eyes glint. She hesitates, but then shakes her head with a sigh. "The path to that planet was lost, all the knowledge is gone along with the previous Navigator. It would take immense effort and resources to rediscover the route. The heir to the von Valancius protectorate must have plenty of other issues to deal with right now. Perhaps later... when the skies above our heads have cleared."

"I hadn't been here that long — just one journey from Footfall and the other journey, the majority of which I spent in the confines of the medbay. I can't tell you much about the first voyage... I was more focused on prayers and ruminations than on the people around me or the journey itself."

“在上一次旅途中，韦尔森总领给我留下了深刻的印象。他当时来过好几次，询问我的健康状况。他是位可敬的人，也是帝国的忠实仆人。他细致地询问了偶然登船的战斗修女的健康状况。我相信，他在检查后勤系统的状况时，肯定也会采取同样细致的态度！”
"During the last journey, Seneschal Werserian stood out for me — he came by several times to ask about my health. He's an honourable man and a loyal servant of the Imperium. I'm surprised she wasn't in league with the cultists. And I'm equally surprised by how deep heresy and treason run in this place..." Argenta frowns and shakes her head. "I'm glad we all made it through that dark hour. May the day that follows be bright!"

“你是从哪里来的？”

I was born in the hold of a warship, grew up following my parents' deployments from one planet to another, and lost my family in the flames of a righteous war."

阿洁塔心不在焉地摸着她腰带上金色双头鹰的碎片。“我的记忆就像一缕青烟，飘荡在死寂的战场上。船上灰色的甲板，军营中严格的生活节奏，还有我母亲的制服——我很喜欢看着它。随后，便是那场战斗……轰隆声，叫喊声，烟尘，士兵们被活活烧死的惨叫声，还有军团的金质双头鹰徽章。它没有沾上烟尘，也没有染上血迹，仿佛是那个走向疯狂的世界中最后一件没被玷污的东西。”
Argenta absent-mindedly touches the fragment of the golden Aquila hanging from her belt. "My memory is like wafts of smoke over a still battlefield. The grey of a ship's plating, the strict cadence of life in military camps. My mother's uniform — I loved looking at it. Then — that battle... the rumbling, the shouting, and the soot. The screams of soldiers burning alive. And the gold of the regiment's Aquila — untouched by soot or blood, the last unsullied piece of a world that was going mad."

“关于我的母亲和我从前的生活，那就是最后的记忆。那个时候，我还没有加入忠嗣学院，没有成为见习修女，没有通过考验，也没有许下誓言。”
"That was my last memory of my mother. And of my former life — before the Schola Progenium and the novitiate, before my trials, before the vows."

"I was one of the best among my peers. And I was selected for the novitiate in the ranks of the Adepta Sororitas. When the hour came, I passed the trials and took my vows. Smoke and soot swallowed the skies and the thousand stars that had once shone over the world."

"Among the handful of survivors was one orphan who had watched all her family die and the garden she'd grown up in burn to ash. There were no more bright stars to be seen... except for one."

"After that she travelled between worlds gripped by turmoil on her ship marked with a silver star and brought hope to the faithful. Numerous accounts confirm this. Her coming helped people turn the tide of the war and wipe away corruption before the Imperium's main forces even arrived."

“几百万人感谢她的救命之恩。然而，当那些异端分子意识到他们的阴谋即将破产时，他们派出了所有的残余部队，追杀那艘带着银星印记的飞船。那艘飞船从空中坠落，落到了某个不知名的世界。关于阿洁塔当时的年纪，并没有确切的记录。在一部分编年史中，她甚至被称为童子圣人，不过这些记录的可信度相当值得怀疑。总之，无论怎样，她并没有活得很久……但她就像落入人间的星星一样，留下了一道明亮的轨迹。”
"Millions of people owed their lives to her. But the heretics, having realised their imminent defeat, sent the remnants of their forces after the ship with the silver star. It fell from the skies onto an obscure world. There are no definitive records of how old Argenta was at the time. In some chronicles she's even called the Child Saint, but their credibility is questionable. Either way, she didn't live long... but she left a bright trail in her wake. Like a falling star."

"Others think that upon falling from the sky, the One Star became a holy chainsword, which Argenta later used to strike down monsters and enemies of the Imperium. Her eyes gleam. "I feel that my undertaking will be fulfilled when I find the answer that has eluded the Ecclesiarchy for millennia! I pray we find the way to Salis Prime soon... The Ruinous Powers must be aligned against us. They stand in the way of faith."

"But not all of Theodora's people have earned my trust. You know who I'm talking about — there is no place for Idira Tlass among the God-Emperor's faithful. I'm surprised she wasn't in league with the cultists. And I'm equally surprised by how deep heresy and treason run in this place..." Argenta frowns and shakes her head. "I'm glad we all made it through that dark hour. May the day that follows be bright!"

I was born in the hold of a warship, grew up following my parents' deployments from one planet to another, and lost my family in the flames of a righteous war."

阿洁塔心不在焉地摸着她腰带上金色双头鹰的碎片。“我的记忆就像一缕青烟，飘荡在死寂的战场上。船上灰色的甲板，军营中严格的生活节奏，还有我母亲的制服——我很喜欢看着它。随后，便是那场战斗……轰隆声，叫喊声，烟尘，士兵们被活活烧死的惨叫声，还有军团的金质双头鹰徽章。它没有沾上烟尘，也没有染上血迹，仿佛是那个走向疯狂的世界中最后一件没被玷污的东西。”
Argenta absent-mindedly touches the fragment of the golden Aquila hanging from her belt. "My memory is like wafts of smoke over a still battlefield. The grey of a ship's plating, the strict cadence of life in military camps. My mother's uniform — I loved looking at it. Then — that battle... the rumbling, the shouting, and the soot. The screams of soldiers burning alive. And the gold of the regiment's Aquila — untouched by soot or blood, the last unsullied piece of a world that was going mad."

“关于我的母亲和我从前的生活，那就是最后的记忆。那个时候，我还没有加入忠嗣学院，没有成为见习修女，没有通过考验，也没有许下誓言。”
"That was my last memory of my mother. And of my former life — before the Schola Progenium and the novitiate, before my trials, before the vows."

"I was one of the best among my peers. And I was selected for the novitiate in the ranks of the Adepta Sororitas. When the hour came, I passed the trials and took my vows. "Among the handful of survivors was one orphan who had watched all her family die and the garden she'd grown up in burn to ash. There were no more bright stars to be seen... except for one."

"After that she travelled between worlds gripped by turmoil on her ship marked with a silver star and brought hope to the faithful. Numerous accounts confirm this. Her coming helped people turn the tide of the war and wipe away corruption before the Imperium's main forces even arrived."

“几百万人感谢她的救命之恩。然而，当那些异端分子意识到他们的阴谋即将破产时，他们派出了所有的残余部队，追杀那艘带着银星印记的飞船。那艘飞船从空中坠落，落到了某个不知名的世界。关于阿洁塔当时的年纪，并没有确切的记录。在一部分编年史中，她甚至被称为童子圣人，不过这些记录的可信度相当值得怀疑。总之，无论怎样，她并没有活得很久……但她就像落入人间的星星一样，留下了一道明亮的轨迹。”
"Millions of people owed their lives to her. But the heretics, having realised their imminent defeat, sent the remnants of their forces after the ship with the silver star. It fell from the skies onto an obscure world. There are no definitive records of how old Argenta was at the time. In some chronicles she's even called the Child Saint, but their credibility is questionable. Either way, she didn't live long... but she left a bright trail in her wake. Like a falling star."

Most of them portrayed Saint Argenta as a girl carrying this banner."

“还有人认为，命运之星从天上掉下来之后，变成了一把神圣的链锯剑。他们认为阿洁塔挥舞着那把链锯剑，击溃了怪物与帝国之敌。而在一部分早期雕刻作品中，阿洁塔的形象是穿着动力装甲的战士，胸前有一颗银色的星星。某种神学理论身为，这件动力装甲正是那件圣遗物。还有一部分人甚至认为，命运之星实际上指的是阿洁塔乘坐的那艘飞船。”
"Others think that upon falling from the sky, the One Star became a holy chainsword, which Argenta later used to strike down monsters and enemies of the Imperium. Some even think that the One Star is actually the ship on which Argenta travelled."

阿洁塔心不在焉地摸着她腰带上金色双头鹰的碎片。“我的记忆就像一缕青烟，飘荡在死寂的战场上。船上灰色的甲板，军营中严格的生活节奏，还有我母亲的制服——我很喜欢看着它。随后，便是那场战斗……轰隆声，叫喊声，烟尘，士兵们被活活烧死的惨叫声，还有军团的金质双头鹰徽章。它没有沾上烟尘，也没有染上血迹，仿佛是那个走向疯狂的世界中最后一件没被玷污的东西。”
Argenta absent-mindedly touches the fragment of the golden Aquila hanging from her belt. "My memory is like wafts of smoke over a still battlefield. The grey of a ship's plating, the strict cadence of life in military camps. My mother's uniform — I loved looking at it. Then — that battle... the rumbling, the shouting, and the soot. The screams of soldiers burning alive. And the gold of the regiment's Aquila — untouched by soot or blood, the last unsullied piece of a world that was going mad."

“关于我的母亲和我从前的生活，那就是最后的记忆。那个时候，我还没有加入忠嗣学院，没有成为见习修女，没有通过考验，也没有许下誓言。”
"That was my last memory of my mother. And of my former life — before the Schola Progenium and the novitiate, before my trials, before the vows."

  • 选择 Choice

“你随身带着的那个金色碎片……”
"That golden shard you carry with you..."

“那是我自己的圣物，是那个军团的双头鹰徽章。或者换个说法，它是在袭击、爆炸与大火中幸存下来的碎片。对我来说，它仿佛是在提醒我——即便是在黑暗的核心，纯洁与光明也依然不会泯灭。”
"My own relic. It's the regiment's Aquila, or rather, the fragment that survived the attack, the explosions, and the fire. For me it's a reminder that purity and radiance can be preserved even in the heart of darkness."

“你是如何成为修女会的一员的？”

“‘成为’……这个词很古怪。虽然听起来没问题，但这个词真的可以用来谈论命定之事吗？如果你问的是我选择的道路本身，那这个问题很容易回答。我像许多其他孤儿一样，在忠嗣学院熬了很多年。那段日子很难熬，但也是我美好的记忆，因为很少有什么能比得上通过试炼之后的满足感。即便试炼会让你的身体因疲惫而疼痛，让你的灵魂在痛苦中抽搐，也无所谓。”
"'Become'... It's such a strange word for it. It seems right, but is that how one talks about their destiny? If you're asking about the path itself — that's easy enough to answer. First, like many other orphans, I endured the Schola Progenium. Those years were rough, but I remember the hardship fondly. Few things can compare with the feeling of satisfaction from a passed trial, even if it leaves your body aching from exhaustion or your soul wincing in pain."

“我是同龄人中的佼佼者，被选为修女会的见习修女。当那重要的时刻到来时，我通过了考验，宣读了我的誓词。那是我人生中最快乐的一天！尽管帝皇的光明一直伴随着我，但全心全意地接受祂的光芒，许下那些誓言时——那简直是一种无与伦比的狂喜。”
"I was one of the best among my peers. And I was selected for the novitiate in the ranks of the Adepta Sororitas. When the hour came, I passed the trials and took my vows. The most joyous day of my life! The Emperor's light has always been with me, but to accept it with all your heart, to utter the oaths — that is a rapture like no other."

The question seems to catch Argenta off guard. "Have I ever...? But that would be shameful weakness, almost heresy! Of course not. I was born for this. I live by the Emperor's will and in His light, I myself am the light, I must be the light — for myself and for those who ask for my protection."

“帝皇选择我来侍奉祂。但除此之外我并不否认——每当我一想到，那些被我射杀的异端分子再也无法让别的孩子沦为孤儿，我就会感到兴奋不已。”
"I was chosen to serve. But beyond that — I won't deny it — few things elate me as much as the thought that the heretic felled by my shot will never again orphan a child."

Argenta bows her head. "It is... my pleasure to be candid."

"If such is the Rogue Trader's wish. Although there isn't much I can tell. I am the Emperor's daughter and His servant... What else is there to know?"

"But one day, the people learned the meaning of darkness. Like a storm, accursed heretics who had sold themselves to the Archenemy descended upon the planet. Smoke and soot swallowed the skies and the thousand stars that had once shone over the world."

“在为数不多的幸存者中，有一个孤儿。她所有家人都死在了她面前，她从小到大长大的花园化为了灰烬。但在她心中，她恪守着绝对的真理，那就是——帝皇会保佑祂的人民。怀着这样的信念，她紧紧地盯着被烟尘覆盖的阴暗天空。可怕的天空中，明亮的星星全都销声匿迹了……只有一颗还在。”
"Among the handful of survivors was one orphan who had watched all her family die and the garden she'd grown up in burn to ash. But in her heart, she knew the absolute truth, just these three words — the Emperor protects. And knowing that, she never looked away from the black, terrifying, smoke-covered sky. There were no more bright stars to be seen... except for one."

“唯一一颗明亮的星星，命运之星，在天空中闪耀着。当那个孤儿对它露出微笑时，命运之星恰好落在了她的手中。那片大陆的所有虔诚之人，都看到了星星落入人间的那一幕。他们认为这是个预兆，前往星星落下的地方。他们团结起来，在命运之星的光芒下，找到了他们的救赎之路。”
"The One Star, the bright star, the silver star shone in the sky. And when the orphan smiled at it — the One Star fell right into her hands. “在那之后，她乘坐着带有银星印记的飞船，穿梭于无数动荡的世界中，给那些世界的虔诚之人带来了希望。许多官方记载都可以证实这样的说法。她的到来帮助当地的人们扭转了战局，让他们赶在帝国主力部队抵达之前就消灭了腐化的痕迹。”
"After that she travelled between worlds gripped by turmoil on her ship marked with a silver star and brought hope to the faithful. Numerous accounts confirm this. Her coming helped people turn the tide of the war and wipe away corruption before the Imperium's main forces even arrived."

“几百万人感谢她的救命之恩。然而，当那些异端分子意识到他们的阴谋即将破产时，他们派出了所有的残余部队，追杀那艘带着银星印记的飞船。那艘飞船从空中坠落，落到了某个不知名的世界。关于阿洁塔当时的年纪，并没有确切的记录。在一部分编年史中，她甚至被称为童子圣人，不过这些记录的可信度相当值得怀疑。总之，无论怎样，她并没有活得很久……但她就像落入人间的星星一样，留下了一道明亮的轨迹。”
"Millions of people owed their lives to her. But the heretics, having realised their imminent defeat, sent the remnants of their forces after the ship with the silver star. It fell from the skies onto an obscure world. There are no definitive records of how old Argenta was at the time. In some chronicles she's even called the Child Saint, but their credibility is questionable. Either way, she didn't live long... but she left a bright trail in her wake. Like a falling star."

“噢，要是我知道那是什么就好了！无论是圣传还是各种传说，都没有给出过明确的答案。古典圣像画师认为，这颗星星变成了一面用银丝织成的旗帜。当这面旗帜被带到战场上时，它会发出明亮的光芒，只会晃瞎异端分子的眼睛，不会伤害虔诚之人。 在绝大部分画师的笔下，圣阿洁塔的形象都是举着旗帜的姑娘。”

Most of them portrayed Saint Argenta as a girl carrying this banner."

“还有人认为，命运之星从天上掉下来之后，变成了一把神圣的链锯剑。他们认为阿洁塔挥舞着那把链锯剑，击溃了怪物与帝国之敌。而在一部分早期雕刻作品中，阿洁塔的形象是穿着动力装甲的战士，胸前有一颗银色的星星。某种神学理论身为，这件动力装甲正是那件圣遗物。还有一部分人甚至认为，命运之星实际上指的是阿洁塔乘坐的那艘飞船。”
"Others think that upon falling from the sky, the One Star became a holy chainsword, which Argenta later used to strike down monsters and enemies of the Imperium. Some even think that the One Star is actually the ship on which Argenta travelled."

Her eyes gleam. "I feel that my undertaking will be fulfilled when I find the answer that has eluded the Ecclesiarchy for millennia! I pray we find the way to Salis Prime soon... The Ruinous Powers must be aligned against us. They stand in the way of faith."

Argenta absent-mindedly touches the fragment of the golden Aquila hanging from her belt. "My memory is like wafts of smoke over a still battlefield. The grey of a ship's plating, the strict cadence of life in military camps. My mother's uniform — I loved looking at it. Then — that battle... the rumbling, the shouting, and the soot. “关于我的母亲和我从前的生活，那就是最后的记忆。那个时候，我还没有加入忠嗣学院，没有成为见习修女，没有通过考验，也没有许下誓言。”

“‘成为’……这个词很古怪。虽然听起来没问题，但这个词真的可以用来谈论命定之事吗？如果你问的是我选择的道路本身，那这个问题很容易回答。我像许多其他孤儿一样，在忠嗣学院熬了很多年。那段日子很难熬，但也是我美好的记忆，因为很少有什么能比得上通过试炼之后的满足感。即便试炼会让你的身体因疲惫而疼痛，让你的灵魂在痛苦中抽搐，也无所谓。”
"'Become'... It's such a strange word for it. It seems right, but is that how one talks about their destiny? If you're asking about the path itself — that's easy enough to answer. First, like many other orphans, I endured the Schola Progenium. Those years were rough, but I remember the hardship fondly. Few things can compare with the feeling of satisfaction from a passed trial, even if it leaves your body aching from exhaustion or your soul wincing in pain."

“我是同龄人中的佼佼者，被选为修女会的见习修女。当那重要的时刻到来时，我通过了考验，宣读了我的誓词。那是我人生中最快乐的一天！尽管帝皇的光明一直伴随着我，但全心全意地接受祂的光芒，许下那些誓言时——那简直是一种无与伦比的狂喜。”
"I was one of the best among my peers. And I was selected for the novitiate in the ranks of the Adepta Sororitas. When the hour came, I passed the trials and took my vows. The most joyous day of my life! The Emperor's light has always been with me, but to accept it with all your heart, to utter the oaths — that is a rapture like no other."

  • 选择 Choice

“你有没有期望过不同的命运？”
"Have you ever wished for a different lot in life?"

这个问题似乎让阿洁塔措手不及。“我有没有期望过……？可那会是可耻的弱点，几乎算是异端邪说！当然没有，我生来就是为了成为修女。我为帝皇的意志而生。在祂的明光中，我也成为了明光。我必须成为明光，这既是为了我自己，也是为了那些寻求我保护的人。”
The question seems to catch Argenta off guard. "Have I ever...? But that would be shameful weakness, almost heresy! Of course not. I was born for this. I live by the Emperor's will and in His light, I myself am the light, I must be the light — for myself and for those who ask for my protection."

“帝皇选择我来侍奉祂。但除此之外我并不否认——每当我一想到，那些被我射杀的异端分子再也无法让别的孩子沦为孤儿，我就会感到兴奋不已。”
"I was chosen to serve. But beyond that — I won't deny it — few things elate me as much as the thought that the heretic felled by my shot will never again orphan a child."

"But one day, the people learned the meaning of darkness. Like a storm, accursed heretics who had sold themselves to the Archenemy descended upon the planet. "Among the handful of survivors was one orphan who had watched all her family die and the garden she'd grown up in burn to ash. There were no more bright stars to be seen... except for one."

"The One Star, the bright star, the silver star shone in the sky. And when the orphan smiled at it — the One Star fell right into her hands. “在那之后，她乘坐着带有银星印记的飞船，穿梭于无数动荡的世界中，给那些世界的虔诚之人带来了希望。许多官方记载都可以证实这样的说法。她的到来帮助当地的人们扭转了战局，让他们赶在帝国主力部队抵达之前就消灭了腐化的痕迹。”
"After that she travelled between worlds gripped by turmoil on her ship marked with a silver star and brought hope to the faithful. Numerous accounts confirm this. Her coming helped people turn the tide of the war and wipe away corruption before the Imperium's main forces even arrived."

“几百万人感谢她的救命之恩。然而，当那些异端分子意识到他们的阴谋即将破产时，他们派出了所有的残余部队，追杀那艘带着银星印记的飞船。那艘飞船从空中坠落，落到了某个不知名的世界。关于阿洁塔当时的年纪，并没有确切的记录。在一部分编年史中，她甚至被称为童子圣人，不过这些记录的可信度相当值得怀疑。总之，无论怎样，她并没有活得很久……但她就像落入人间的星星一样，留下了一道明亮的轨迹。”
"Millions of people owed their lives to her. But the heretics, having realised their imminent defeat, sent the remnants of their forces after the ship with the silver star. It fell from the skies onto an obscure world. There are no definitive records of how old Argenta was at the time. In some chronicles she's even called the Child Saint, but their credibility is questionable. Either way, she didn't live long... but she left a bright trail in her wake. Like a falling star."

Most of them portrayed Saint Argenta as a girl carrying this banner."

“还有人认为，命运之星从天上掉下来之后，变成了一把神圣的链锯剑。他们认为阿洁塔挥舞着那把链锯剑，击溃了怪物与帝国之敌。而在一部分早期雕刻作品中，阿洁塔的形象是穿着动力装甲的战士，胸前有一颗银色的星星。某种神学理论身为，这件动力装甲正是那件圣遗物。还有一部分人甚至认为，命运之星实际上指的是阿洁塔乘坐的那艘飞船。”
"Others think that upon falling from the sky, the One Star became a holy chainsword, which Argenta later used to strike down monsters and enemies of the Imperium. "I beg your pardon, Rogue Trader. Here I am, talking about what every lesser noble in the Imperium knows! So what exactly are you interested in hearing about?"

Argenta absent-mindedly touches the fragment of the golden Aquila hanging from her belt. "My memory is like wafts of smoke over a still battlefield. "But one day, the people learned the meaning of darkness. Like a storm, accursed heretics who had sold themselves to the Archenemy descended upon the planet. "Among the handful of survivors was one orphan who had watched all her family die and the garden she'd grown up in burn to ash. But in her heart, she knew the absolute truth, just these three words — the Emperor protects. And knowing that, she never looked away from the black, terrifying, smoke-covered sky. There were no more bright stars to be seen... except for one."

“唯一一颗明亮的星星，命运之星，在天空中闪耀着。当那个孤儿对它露出微笑时，命运之星恰好落在了她的手中。那片大陆的所有虔诚之人，都看到了星星落入人间的那一幕。他们认为这是个预兆，前往星星落下的地方。他们团结起来，在命运之星的光芒下，找到了他们的救赎之路。”
"The One Star, the bright star, the silver star shone in the sky. And when the orphan smiled at it — the One Star fell right into her hands. "After that she travelled between worlds gripped by turmoil on her ship marked with a silver star and brought hope to the faithful. Numerous accounts confirm this. Her coming helped people turn the tide of the war and wipe away corruption before the Imperium's main forces even arrived."

"Millions of people owed their lives to her. But the heretics, having realised their imminent defeat, sent the remnants of their forces after the ship with the silver star. It fell from the skies onto an obscure world. There are no definitive records of how old Argenta was at the time. In some chronicles she's even called the Child Saint, but their credibility is questionable. Either way, she didn't live long... but she left a bright trail in her wake. Like a falling star."

“还有人认为，命运之星从天上掉下来之后，变成了一把神圣的链锯剑。他们认为阿洁塔挥舞着那把链锯剑，击溃了怪物与帝国之敌。而在一部分早期雕刻作品中，阿洁塔的形象是穿着动力装甲的战士，胸前有一颗银色的星星。某种神学理论身为，这件动力装甲正是那件圣遗物。还有一部分人甚至认为，命运之星实际上指的是阿洁塔乘坐的那艘飞船。”
"Others think that upon falling from the sky, the One Star became a holy chainsword, which Argenta later used to strike down monsters and enemies of the Imperium. “她们只穿长袍，不着盔甲，手里拿着开膛剑。那些姐妹曾在信仰的道路上踌躇不前，她们会在战场上找到救赎。尽管她们通常活不了多久，但以赎罪之名而死，总比带着阴影活着要好。”
"Wearing nothing but robes, no armour, Eviscerator in hand, those sisters who have once faltered find repentance on the battlefield. Their lives are seldom long, but a death in the name of purgation is a better fate than to live with a shadow in one's soul."

"And we seek out the relics that have been lost. Neither a coven of heretics nor the most wicked death world can deter Sisters Pronatus when their goal is to return a piece of the great legacy of the Imperium into the hands of the faithful."

After a short pause, Argenta adds with somewhat arrogant haste, "And my order has all the more reason to be known for the martial prowess of its sisters. We are the keepers of the Imperium's relics! What would become of our blessed heroes' legacy if the Sisters Pronatus could not protect it?"

Lady Theodora came to my aid and brought me aboard her ship, where her crew attended to me in my weakened state. It all happened not too long ago — I had barely recovered from my wounds when the cultists struck. Truly the servants of evil know no rest! There is no place where we can be safe from their machinations."

阿洁塔心不在焉地摸着她腰带上金色双头鹰的碎片。“我的记忆就像一缕青烟，飘荡在死寂的战场上。船上灰色的甲板，军营中严格的生活节奏，还有我母亲的制服——我很喜欢看着它。随后，便是那场战斗……轰隆声，叫喊声，烟尘，士兵们被活活烧死的惨叫声，还有军团的金质双头鹰徽章。它没有沾上烟尘，也没有染上血迹，仿佛是那个走向疯狂的世界中最后一件没被玷污的东西。”
Argenta absent-mindedly touches the fragment of the golden Aquila hanging from her belt. "My memory is like wafts of smoke over a still battlefield. The grey of a ship's plating, the strict cadence of life in military camps. My mother's uniform — I loved looking at it. Then — that battle... the rumbling, the shouting, and the soot. The screams of soldiers burning alive. And the gold of the regiment's Aquila — untouched by soot or blood, the last unsullied piece of a world that was going mad."

“关于我的母亲和我从前的生活，那就是最后的记忆。那个时候，我还没有加入忠嗣学院，没有成为见习修女，没有通过考验，也没有许下誓言。”
"That was my last memory of my mother. And of my former life — before the Schola Progenium and the novitiate, before my trials, before the vows."

"But one day, the people learned the meaning of darkness. Like a storm, accursed heretics who had sold themselves to the Archenemy descended upon the planet. Shells flew from the sky that desolated whole cities, and burned the gardens, and filled the riverbeds with the blood of the faithful. Smoke and soot swallowed the skies and the thousand stars that had once shone over the world."

“在为数不多的幸存者中，有一个孤儿。她所有家人都死在了她面前，她从小到大长大的花园化为了灰烬。但在她心中，她恪守着绝对的真理，那就是——帝皇会保佑祂的人民。怀着这样的信念，她紧紧地盯着被烟尘覆盖的阴暗天空。可怕的天空中，明亮的星星全都销声匿迹了……只有一颗还在。”
"Among the handful of survivors was one orphan who had watched all her family die and the garden she'd grown up in burn to ash. But in her heart, she knew the absolute truth, just these three words — the Emperor protects. And knowing that, she never looked away from the black, terrifying, smoke-covered sky. There were no more bright stars to be seen... except for one."

“唯一一颗明亮的星星，命运之星，在天空中闪耀着。当那个孤儿对它露出微笑时，命运之星恰好落在了她的手中。那片大陆的所有虔诚之人，都看到了星星落入人间的那一幕。他们认为这是个预兆，前往星星落下的地方。他们团结起来，在命运之星的光芒下，找到了他们的救赎之路。”
"The One Star, the bright star, the silver star shone in the sky. And when the orphan smiled at it — the One Star fell right into her hands. All the faithful in every corner of the continent who saw the trail of the falling star recognised it as an omen and went looking for the place where it landed. And they rallied together, and with the light of the One Star, they found their salvation."

“这个故事里的女孩就是圣阿洁塔吗？”
"The girl from the story — that was Saint Argenta?"

“没错，那就是她传奇生涯的开端。众所周知，她生活的世界遭遇了动荡，那个世界的异端分子发动了一场可怕的叛乱。他们消灭了整颗行星上的所有生命——除了阿洁塔靠着命运之星与信仰的力量救下来的那些人。”
"Yes. That was the beginning of her hagiography. It is known that she lived on a world where heretics staged a terrible insurrection. They wiped out all life on the planet — except those whom Saint Argenta managed to save with the One Star. And with the strength of her faith."

“在那之后，她乘坐着带有银星印记的飞船，穿梭于无数动荡的世界中，给那些世界的虔诚之人带来了希望。许多官方记载都可以证实这样的说法。她的到来帮助当地的人们扭转了战局，让他们赶在帝国主力部队抵达之前就消灭了腐化的痕迹。”
"After that she travelled between worlds gripped by turmoil on her ship marked with a silver star and brought hope to the faithful. Numerous accounts confirm this. Her coming helped people turn the tide of the war and wipe away corruption before the Imperium's main forces even arrived."

“几百万人感谢她的救命之恩。然而，当那些异端分子意识到他们的阴谋即将破产时，他们派出了所有的残余部队，追杀那艘带着银星印记的飞船。那艘飞船从空中坠落，落到了某个不知名的世界。关于阿洁塔当时的年纪，并没有确切的记录。在一部分编年史中，她甚至被称为童子圣人，不过这些记录的可信度相当值得怀疑。总之，无论怎样，她并没有活得很久……但她就像落入人间的星星一样，留下了一道明亮的轨迹。”
"Millions of people owed their lives to her. But the heretics, having realised their imminent defeat, sent the remnants of their forces after the ship with the silver star. It fell from the skies onto an obscure world. There are no definitive records of how old Argenta was at the time. In some chronicles she's even called the Child Saint, but their credibility is questionable. Either way, she didn't live long... but she left a bright trail in her wake. Like a falling star."

“噢，要是我知道那是什么就好了！无论是圣传还是各种传说，都没有给出过明确的答案。古典圣像画师认为，这颗星星变成了一面用银丝织成的旗帜。当这面旗帜被带到战场上时，它会发出明亮的光芒，只会晃瞎异端分子的眼睛，不会伤害虔诚之人。 在绝大部分画师的笔下，圣阿洁塔的形象都是举着旗帜的姑娘。”
"Oh, if I only knew! Neither the hagiography nor the legends give a straight answer. Classical iconographers believed that the star turned into a banner woven from silver thread, which, when brought onto the battlefield, would shed light that blinded only heretics but did no harm to the faithful. Most of them portrayed Saint Argenta as a girl carrying this banner."

“还有人认为，命运之星从天上掉下来之后，变成了一把神圣的链锯剑。他们认为阿洁塔挥舞着那把链锯剑，击溃了怪物与帝国之敌。而在一部分早期雕刻作品中，阿洁塔的形象是穿着动力装甲的战士，胸前有一颗银色的星星。某种神学理论身为，这件动力装甲正是那件圣遗物。还有一部分人甚至认为，命运之星实际上指的是阿洁塔乘坐的那艘飞船。”
"Others think that upon falling from the sky, the One Star became a holy chainsword, which Argenta later used to strike down monsters and enemies of the Imperium. In some of the earlier engravings, Argenta is depicted wearing power armour with a silver star on her chest — one theological theory suggests that this armour was, in fact, the relic. Some even think that the One Star is actually the ship on which Argenta travelled."

她的双眼闪闪发光。“这个问题几千年来一直在困扰着国教。我认为，当我找到这个问题的答案时，就完成了我的使命！我祈祷我们能尽快找到通往萨利斯主星的航路……毁灭之力肯定会联合起来阻止我们，他们肯定会阻挡信仰的道路。”
Her eyes gleam. "I feel that my undertaking will be fulfilled when I find the answer that has eluded the Ecclesiarchy for millennia! I pray we find the way to Salis Prime soon... The Ruinous Powers must be aligned against us. They stand in the way of faith."

阿洁塔顿了顿，声音中带着些许傲慢，急匆匆地补充道。“至于我所在的修会，更是以修女高超的武艺而闻名。我们可是帝国圣物的守护者！如果连普罗图斯修女都无法守护这些圣物，那些受祝福的英雄遗物会变成什么样子？”
After a short pause, Argenta adds with somewhat arrogant haste, "And my order has all the more reason to be known for the martial prowess of its sisters. We are the keepers of the Imperium's relics! What would become of our blessed heroes' legacy if the Sisters Pronatus could not protect it?"

  • 选择 Choice

“你刚刚说，你的修会属于卡利西斯分支，那你为什么会来科罗努斯扩区？”
"You said you belong to the Calixian branch of your order. What brought you to the Koronus Expanse?"

“是修会派我来落脚港的，我的任务是协助当地的德鲁苏斯修会，守护神圣的圣骨匣。这个圣骨匣早在落脚港创始人帕西姆斯·德维恩的时代，就已经放在那里了。”
"The order sent me to Footfall. My undertaking was to assist the local priesthood of Drusians in caring for a sacred reliquary that had been there since the time of Parsimus Dewain, the station's founder."

  • 选择 Choice

"Are there any other members of the Adepta Sororitas in the Koronus Expanse?"

“据我所知没有，但修女会有很多修会，每个修会都可以独立运作，将她们的修女送到国教认为该去的地方。或许我的姐妹们此刻正在大审判官身边履行她们的职责？愿神皇祝福她们的道路。我希望会是这样，如果能与她们一起祈祷、一起训练，哪怕只有一个晚上的时间，也会令我快乐无比！”
"None that I'm aware of, but the Sisterhood's orders are many and can operate independently of one another, sending their sisters wherever their presence is needed as deemed by the Ecclesiarchy. Perhaps somewhere in the Lord Inquisitor's retinue, may his path be blessed, my sisters perform their duty as we speak? I wish it were so — even a single evening spent in joint prayer and training would bring me joy!"

“关于修女会，我没有别的问题要问了。”
"I have no more questions about the Sisterhood."

“如果你还有别的问题要问，无须藏在心里，这并不合适！对神圣之物感兴趣是一种美德。”
"Should any more arise — keeping them to yourself would be imprudent! It is a virtue to take an interest in holiness."

"About me?" She looks surprised. "I am the Emperor's daughter and His servant. What else is there to tell about me?"

  • 选择 Choice

“你是怎么上了西奥多拉的船？”
"How did you end up on Theodora's ship?"

阿洁塔的表情明显变得黯淡下来。“我第一次上她的船，是为了从落脚港前往某颗偏僻的行星。但我猜，你感兴趣的并不是我的第一次旅行，而是在异端分子袭击之前，我出于什么原因上了她的船。这个故事很复杂，我当时只是碰巧……”她突然顿住了。
Argenta's expression darkens visibly. "I first came here when I found myself in need of passage from Footfall to a remote planet. But I imagine what interests you is not that first journey, but rather what brought me aboard prior to the cultist attack. That story is complicated. It just so happened that I..." She stops short.

“我当时犯了个错误。我一时懈怠，遭到了混沌大敌邪恶仆从的伏击。我受了重伤，西奥多拉夫人前来救援。她把我带到了她的船上，让她的船员照顾虚弱不堪的我。这一切就发生在不久之前，因为那些异端分子袭击的时候，我的伤势几乎还没恢复过来。说真的，那些邪恶的仆从简直是一刻不停地筹谋！根本没有任何地方可以免遭他们的阴谋所害。”
"I made a mistake. In a moment of laxity, I was ambushed by the accursed followers of the Archenemy. I was badly wounded. Lady Theodora came to my aid and brought me aboard her ship, where her crew attended to me in my weakened state. It all happened not too long ago — I had barely recovered from my wounds when the cultists struck. Truly the servants of evil know no rest! There is no place where we can be safe from their machinations."

"Sadly, they did not. Lady Theodora was in a hurry and chose not to stay on the planet. Her people took me to her ship while I was unconscious, and when I came to my senses, we were already flying away. Oh, how I pray to come face to face with those heretics once more! And it's bound to happen someday."

  • 选择 Choice

"It happens even to the best of us!" Argenta says heatedly. Then she frowns and lowers her head for a moment. "My mistakes are my burden to bear. I'll find a way to atone for them."

"On one of the recently discovered planets in the Expanse. No one suspected that it had already been tainted by the filth of heresy. Had I known it beforehand — of course I would have been on my guard."

Argenta's eyes glint. She hesitates, but then shakes her head with a sigh. "The path to that planet was lost, all the knowledge is gone along with the previous Navigator. It would take immense effort and resources to rediscover the route. The heir to the von Valancius protectorate must have plenty of other issues to deal with right now. Perhaps later... when the skies above our heads have cleared."

  • 选择 Choice

"What was it like travelling on Theodora's ship?"

“我在这里没呆太久，仅仅是离开了落脚港一趟，还有另一趟旅行。我绝大部分时间都是在医疗甲板上度过的。第一次航行的情形，我恐怕已经不太记得了……我当时绝大部分时间都是在专注地祈祷、冥想，没太在意周围的人，也没太在意那场旅途本身。”
"I hadn't been here that long — just one journey from Footfall and the other journey, the majority of which I spent in the confines of the medbay. I can't tell you much about the first voyage... I was more focused on prayers and ruminations than on the people around me or the journey itself."

“在上一次旅途中，韦尔森总领给我留下了深刻的印象。他当时来过好几次，询问我的健康状况。他是位可敬的人，也是帝国的忠实仆人。他细致地询问了偶然登船的战斗修女的健康状况。我相信，他在检查后勤系统的状况时，肯定也会采取同样细致的态度！”
"During the last journey, Seneschal Werserian stood out for me — he came by several times to ask about my health. He's an honourable man and a loyal servant of the Imperium. “不过，并非西奥多拉所有的船员都赢得了我的信任。你知道我指的是谁，神皇忠诚的信徒之中，没有伊迪拉·特拉斯的位置。她居然没和异端分子厮混在一起，真是让我惊讶。这个地方滋生着无数异端与叛国行为，这也同样让我惊讶……”阿洁塔皱着眉头，摇了摇头。“我很高兴我们顺利度过了那黑暗的时刻。愿接下来的日子里，光明与我们同在！”

I'm surprised she wasn't in league with the cultists. And I'm equally surprised by how deep heresy and treason run in this place..." Argenta frowns and shakes her head. "I'm glad we all made it through that dark hour. May the day that follows be bright!"

“你是从哪里来的？”
"Where do you hail from?"

“现在我可以告诉你了。我来自银河系各地，但我并没有故乡。我……”阿洁塔的眼神黯淡了片刻。“我的父母都是帝国卫队的军官。我出生在战舰的船舱里，跟随我父母的调度，不断地在各个行星之间辗转往复，就这样长大成人。后来，爆发了一场正义的战争，而我的家人被烈焰吞噬了。”
"Now that I can tell you. I come from everywhere and nowhere. I..." Argenta's eyes darken for a moment. "I am the child of officers of the Imperial Guard. I was born in the hold of a warship, grew up following my parents' deployments from one planet to another, and lost my family in the flames of a righteous war."

阿洁塔心不在焉地摸着她腰带上金色双头鹰的碎片。“我的记忆就像一缕青烟，飘荡在死寂的战场上。船上灰色的甲板，军营中严格的生活节奏，还有我母亲的制服——我很喜欢看着它。随后，便是那场战斗……轰隆声，叫喊声，烟尘，士兵们被活活烧死的惨叫声，还有军团的金质双头鹰徽章。它没有沾上烟尘，也没有染上血迹，仿佛是那个走向疯狂的世界中最后一件没被玷污的东西。”
Argenta absent-mindedly touches the fragment of the golden Aquila hanging from her belt. "My memory is like wafts of smoke over a still battlefield. The grey of a ship's plating, the strict cadence of life in military camps. My mother's uniform — I loved looking at it. Then — that battle... the rumbling, the shouting, and the soot. The screams of soldiers burning alive. And the gold of the regiment's Aquila — untouched by soot or blood, the last unsullied piece of a world that was going mad."

“关于我的母亲和我从前的生活，那就是最后的记忆。那个时候，我还没有加入忠嗣学院，没有成为见习修女，没有通过考验，也没有许下誓言。”
"That was my last memory of my mother. And of my former life — before the Schola Progenium and the novitiate, before my trials, before the vows."

"My own relic. It's the regiment's Aquila, or rather, the fragment that survived the attack, the explosions, and the fire. For me it's a reminder that purity and radiance can be preserved even in the heart of darkness."

“你是如何成为修女会的一员的？”

"'Become'... It's such a strange word for it. It seems right, but is that how one talks about their destiny? If you're asking about the path itself — that's easy enough to answer. First, like many other orphans, I endured the Schola Progenium. Those years were rough, but I remember the hardship fondly. Few things can compare with the feeling of satisfaction from a passed trial, even if it leaves your body aching from exhaustion or your soul wincing in pain."

“我是同龄人中的佼佼者，被选为修女会的见习修女。当那重要的时刻到来时，我通过了考验，宣读了我的誓词。那是我人生中最快乐的一天！尽管帝皇的光明一直伴随着我，但全心全意地接受祂的光芒，许下那些誓言时——那简直是一种无与伦比的狂喜。”
"I was one of the best among my peers. And I was selected for the novitiate in the ranks of the Adepta Sororitas. When the hour came, I passed the trials and took my vows. The most joyous day of my life! The Emperor's light has always been with me, but to accept it with all your heart, to utter the oaths — that is a rapture like no other."

  • 选择 Choice

“你有没有期望过不同的命运？”

这个问题似乎让阿洁塔措手不及。“我有没有期望过……？可那会是可耻的弱点，几乎算是异端邪说！当然没有，我生来就是为了成为修女。我为帝皇的意志而生。在祂的明光中，我也成为了明光。我必须成为明光，这既是为了我自己，也是为了那些寻求我保护的人。”
The question seems to catch Argenta off guard. "Have I ever...? But that would be shameful weakness, almost heresy! Of course not. I was born for this. I live by the Emperor's will and in His light, I myself am the light, I must be the light — for myself and for those who ask for my protection."

“帝皇选择我来侍奉祂。但除此之外我并不否认——每当我一想到，那些被我射杀的异端分子再也无法让别的孩子沦为孤儿，我就会感到兴奋不已。”
"I was chosen to serve. But beyond that — I won't deny it — few things elate me as much as the thought that the heretic felled by my shot will never again orphan a child."

"Gladly! Listen..." She begins her tale, her eyes half-closed and her voice almost singing: "Long ago, there was a blessed world. Thousands of stars covered the sky there, so bright that its denizens hardly knew the darkness of night. Thousands of rivers nurtured the soil, thousands of gardens bloomed every spring, and at every moment, thousands of prayers were flying into the clear air, thanking and praising the Emperor."

“但突然有一天，人们明白了黑暗的含义。一大群该死的异端分子仿佛风暴一样降临到了这颗行星，他们将灵魂出卖给了混沌大敌。炮弹从天而降，城市被夷平，花园被烧毁，河里流满了虔诚之人的鲜血。硝烟与烟尘遮天蔽日，吞没了曾经照亮这个世界的群星。”
"But one day, the people learned the meaning of darkness. Like a storm, accursed heretics who had sold themselves to the Archenemy descended upon the planet. Shells flew from the sky that desolated whole cities, and burned the gardens, and filled the riverbeds with the blood of the faithful. Smoke and soot swallowed the skies and the thousand stars that had once shone over the world."

“在为数不多的幸存者中，有一个孤儿。她所有家人都死在了她面前，她从小到大长大的花园化为了灰烬。但在她心中，她恪守着绝对的真理，那就是——帝皇会保佑祂的人民。怀着这样的信念，她紧紧地盯着被烟尘覆盖的阴暗天空。可怕的天空中，明亮的星星全都销声匿迹了……只有一颗还在。”
"Among the handful of survivors was one orphan who had watched all her family die and the garden she'd grown up in burn to ash. But in her heart, she knew the absolute truth, just these three words — the Emperor protects. And knowing that, she never looked away from the black, terrifying, smoke-covered sky. There were no more bright stars to be seen... except for one."

“唯一一颗明亮的星星，命运之星，在天空中闪耀着。当那个孤儿对它露出微笑时，命运之星恰好落在了她的手中。那片大陆的所有虔诚之人，都看到了星星落入人间的那一幕。他们认为这是个预兆，前往星星落下的地方。他们团结起来，在命运之星的光芒下，找到了他们的救赎之路。”
"The One Star, the bright star, the silver star shone in the sky. And when the orphan smiled at it — the One Star fell right into her hands. All the faithful in every corner of the continent who saw the trail of the falling star recognised it as an omen and went looking for the place where it landed. And they rallied together, and with the light of the One Star, they found their salvation."

  • 选择 Choice

“这个故事里的女孩就是圣阿洁塔吗？”
"The girl from the story — that was Saint Argenta?"

“没错，那就是她传奇生涯的开端。众所周知，她生活的世界遭遇了动荡，那个世界的异端分子发动了一场可怕的叛乱。他们消灭了整颗行星上的所有生命——除了阿洁塔靠着命运之星与信仰的力量救下来的那些人。”
"Yes. That was the beginning of her hagiography. It is known that she lived on a world where heretics staged a terrible insurrection. They wiped out all life on the planet — except those whom Saint Argenta managed to save with the One Star. And with the strength of her faith."

“在那之后，她乘坐着带有银星印记的飞船，穿梭于无数动荡的世界中，给那些世界的虔诚之人带来了希望。许多官方记载都可以证实这样的说法。她的到来帮助当地的人们扭转了战局，让他们赶在帝国主力部队抵达之前就消灭了腐化的痕迹。”
"After that she travelled between worlds gripped by turmoil on her ship marked with a silver star and brought hope to the faithful. Numerous accounts confirm this. Her coming helped people turn the tide of the war and wipe away corruption before the Imperium's main forces even arrived."

“几百万人感谢她的救命之恩。然而，当那些异端分子意识到他们的阴谋即将破产时，他们派出了所有的残余部队，追杀那艘带着银星印记的飞船。那艘飞船从空中坠落，落到了某个不知名的世界。关于阿洁塔当时的年纪，并没有确切的记录。在一部分编年史中，她甚至被称为童子圣人，不过这些记录的可信度相当值得怀疑。总之，无论怎样，她并没有活得很久……但她就像落入人间的星星一样，留下了一道明亮的轨迹。”
"Millions of people owed their lives to her. But the heretics, having realised their imminent defeat, sent the remnants of their forces after the ship with the silver star. It fell from the skies onto an obscure world. There are no definitive records of how old Argenta was at the time. In some chronicles she's even called the Child Saint, but their credibility is questionable. Either way, she didn't live long... but she left a bright trail in her wake. Like a falling star."

  • 选择 Choice

"So what is this One Star?"

“噢，要是我知道那是什么就好了！无论是圣传还是各种传说，都没有给出过明确的答案。古典圣像画师认为，这颗星星变成了一面用银丝织成的旗帜。当这面旗帜被带到战场上时，它会发出明亮的光芒，只会晃瞎异端分子的眼睛，不会伤害虔诚之人。 在绝大部分画师的笔下，圣阿洁塔的形象都是举着旗帜的姑娘。”
"Oh, if I only knew! Neither the hagiography nor the legends give a straight answer. Classical iconographers believed that the star turned into a banner woven from silver thread, which, when brought onto the battlefield, would shed light that blinded only heretics but did no harm to the faithful. Most of them portrayed Saint Argenta as a girl carrying this banner."

“还有人认为，命运之星从天上掉下来之后，变成了一把神圣的链锯剑。他们认为阿洁塔挥舞着那把链锯剑，击溃了怪物与帝国之敌。而在一部分早期雕刻作品中，阿洁塔的形象是穿着动力装甲的战士，胸前有一颗银色的星星。某种神学理论身为，这件动力装甲正是那件圣遗物。还有一部分人甚至认为，命运之星实际上指的是阿洁塔乘坐的那艘飞船。”
"Others think that upon falling from the sky, the One Star became a holy chainsword, which Argenta later used to strike down monsters and enemies of the Imperium. In some of the earlier engravings, Argenta is depicted wearing power armour with a silver star on her chest — one theological theory suggests that this armour was, in fact, the relic. Some even think that the One Star is actually the ship on which Argenta travelled."

她的双眼闪闪发光。“这个问题几千年来一直在困扰着国教。我认为，当我找到这个问题的答案时，就完成了我的使命！我祈祷我们能尽快找到通往萨利斯主星的航路……毁灭之力肯定会联合起来阻止我们，他们肯定会阻挡信仰的道路。”
Her eyes gleam. "I feel that my undertaking will be fulfilled when I find the answer that has eluded the Ecclesiarchy for millennia! I pray we find the way to Salis Prime soon... The Ruinous Powers must be aligned against us. They stand in the way of faith."

“如果你还有别的问题要问，无须藏在心里，这并不合适！对神圣之物感兴趣是一种美德。”
"Should any more arise — keeping them to yourself would be imprudent! It is a virtue to take an interest in holiness."

  • 选择 Choice

“和我说说你自己的事情吧。”
"Tell me about yourself."

“我自己的事情？”她看起来很惊讶。“我是帝皇的女儿，也是祂的仆人。关于我，还有什么可说的？”
"About me?" She looks surprised. "I am the Emperor's daughter and His servant. What else is there to tell about me?"

  • 选择 Choice

“你是怎么上了西奥多拉的船？”
"How did you end up on Theodora's ship?"

阿洁塔的表情明显变得黯淡下来。“我第一次上她的船，是为了从落脚港前往某颗偏僻的行星。但我猜，你感兴趣的并不是我的第一次旅行，而是在异端分子袭击之前，我出于什么原因上了她的船。这个故事很复杂，我当时只是碰巧……”她突然顿住了。
Argenta's expression darkens visibly. "I first came here when I found myself in need of passage from Footfall to a remote planet. But I imagine what interests you is not that first journey, but rather what brought me aboard prior to the cultist attack. That story is complicated. It just so happened that I..." She stops short.

“我当时犯了个错误。我一时懈怠，遭到了混沌大敌邪恶仆从的伏击。我受了重伤，西奥多拉夫人前来救援。她把我带到了她的船上，让她的船员照顾虚弱不堪的我。这一切就发生在不久之前，因为那些异端分子袭击的时候，我的伤势几乎还没恢复过来。说真的，那些邪恶的仆从简直是一刻不停地筹谋！根本没有任何地方可以免遭他们的阴谋所害。”
"I made a mistake. In a moment of laxity, I was ambushed by the accursed followers of the Archenemy. I was badly wounded. Lady Theodora came to my aid and brought me aboard her ship, where her crew attended to me in my weakened state. It all happened not too long ago — I had barely recovered from my wounds when the cultists struck. Truly the servants of evil know no rest! There is no place where we can be safe from their machinations."

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice

“那些打伤你的人怎么样了？西奥多拉的人消灭他们了吗？”
"What happened to the people who wounded you? Did Theodora's men eliminate them?"

“遗憾的是，那些敌人并没有被消灭。西奥多拉夫人当时很着急，没有继续在那颗行星上停留。当我不省人事的时候，她的人把我带到了船上，而当我醒过来的时候，我们早已飞走了。噢，我真希望能再次面对那些异端分子！总有一天，我会再次面对他们。”
"Sadly, they did not. Lady Theodora was in a hurry and chose not to stay on the planet. Her people took me to her ship while I was unconscious, and when I came to my senses, we were already flying away. Oh, how I pray to come face to face with those heretics once more! And it's bound to happen someday."

  • 选择 Choice

“让你承认犯了错误就这么难吗？”
"Is it difficult for you to accept that you made a mistake?"

“就算是我们之中最出色的人，也难免会犯错误！”阿洁塔激愤地说道，随后她皱起眉头，低下了头。“我的错误是我肩上的重担，我会想办法赎罪的。”
"It happens even to the best of us!" Argenta says heatedly. Then she frowns and lowers her head for a moment. "My mistakes are my burden to bear. I'll find a way to atone for them."

  • 选择 Choice

“这件事情是在什么地方发生的？”
"Where did this happen?"

“是在科罗努斯扩区最近才发现的行星，根本没人想到它早已被异端分子玷污。如果我当时知道这件事情的话，我肯定会提高警惕。”
"On one of the recently discovered planets in the Expanse. No one suspected that it had already been tainted by the filth of heresy. Had I known it beforehand — of course I would have been on my guard."

  • 选择 Choice

“我们可以去那颗行星，收拾那些崇拜混沌的异端分子。”
"We could go to that planet and deal with the Chaos worshippers."

阿洁塔的眼睛亮了起来。她犹豫了一会儿，随后叹息着摇了摇头。“通往那颗行星的航道已经找不到了。随着前任导航者的离世，我们所有的知识都遗落了。想要重新找到这条航道，恐怕要耗费大量人力与资源。冯·瓦兰修斯王朝的继承人肯定有很多别的问题急需处理。或许过些日子……等到我们头上的天空放晴之后再说也不迟。”
Argenta's eyes glint. She hesitates, but then shakes her head with a sigh. "The path to that planet was lost, all the knowledge is gone along with the previous Navigator. It would take immense effort and resources to rediscover the route. The heir to the von Valancius protectorate must have plenty of other issues to deal with right now. Perhaps later... when the skies above our heads have cleared."

  • 选择 Choice

“在西奥多拉的船上旅行是怎样的感觉？”
"What was it like travelling on Theodora's ship?"

“我在这里没呆太久，仅仅是离开了落脚港一趟，还有另一趟旅行。我绝大部分时间都是在医疗甲板上度过的。第一次航行的情形，我恐怕已经不太记得了……我当时绝大部分时间都是在专注地祈祷、冥想，没太在意周围的人，也没太在意那场旅途本身。”
"I hadn't been here that long — just one journey from Footfall and the other journey, the majority of which I spent in the confines of the medbay. I can't tell you much about the first voyage... I was more focused on prayers and ruminations than on the people around me or the journey itself."

“在上一次旅途中，韦尔森总领给我留下了深刻的印象。他当时来过好几次，询问我的健康状况。他是位可敬的人，也是帝国的忠实仆人。他细致地询问了偶然登船的战斗修女的健康状况。我相信，他在检查后勤系统的状况时，肯定也会采取同样细致的态度！”
"During the last journey, Seneschal Werserian stood out for me — he came by several times to ask about my health. He's an honourable man and a loyal servant of the Imperium. I think he is as meticulous in his inspections of the logistics systems as he is in his enquiries about the health of the occasional Sister of Battle aboard the ship!"

“不过，并非西奥多拉所有的船员都赢得了我的信任。你知道我指的是谁，神皇忠诚的信徒之中，没有伊迪拉·特拉斯的位置。她居然没和异端分子厮混在一起，真是让我惊讶。这个地方滋生着无数异端与叛国行为，这也同样让我惊讶……”阿洁塔皱着眉头，摇了摇头。“我很高兴我们顺利度过了那黑暗的时刻。愿接下来的日子里，光明与我们同在！”
"But not all of Theodora's people have earned my trust. You know who I'm talking about — there is no place for Idira Tlass among the God-Emperor's faithful. I'm surprised she wasn't in league with the cultists. And I'm equally surprised by how deep heresy and treason run in this place..." Argenta frowns and shakes her head. "I'm glad we all made it through that dark hour. May the day that follows be bright!"

"I don't have any more questions, thank you."

“没问题。”
"As you wish."

“你准备好告诉我更多你自己的事情了吗？”

"If such is the Rogue Trader's wish. Although there isn't much I can tell. I am the Emperor's daughter and His servant... What else is there to know?"

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice

“你是从哪里来的？”
"Where do you hail from?"

“现在我可以告诉你了。我来自银河系各地，但我并没有故乡。我……”阿洁塔的眼神黯淡了片刻。“我的父母都是帝国卫队的军官。我出生在战舰的船舱里，跟随我父母的调度，不断地在各个行星之间辗转往复，就这样长大成人。后来，爆发了一场正义的战争，而我的家人被烈焰吞噬了。”
"Now that I can tell you. I come from everywhere and nowhere. I..." Argenta's eyes darken for a moment. "I am the child of officers of the Imperial Guard. I was born in the hold of a warship, grew up following my parents' deployments from one planet to another, and lost my family in the flames of a righteous war."

阿洁塔心不在焉地摸着她腰带上金色双头鹰的碎片。“我的记忆就像一缕青烟，飘荡在死寂的战场上。船上灰色的甲板，军营中严格的生活节奏，还有我母亲的制服——我很喜欢看着它。随后，便是那场战斗……轰隆声，叫喊声，烟尘，士兵们被活活烧死的惨叫声，还有军团的金质双头鹰徽章。它没有沾上烟尘，也没有染上血迹，仿佛是那个走向疯狂的世界中最后一件没被玷污的东西。”
Argenta absent-mindedly touches the fragment of the golden Aquila hanging from her belt. "My memory is like wafts of smoke over a still battlefield. The grey of a ship's plating, the strict cadence of life in military camps. My mother's uniform — I loved looking at it. Then — that battle... the rumbling, the shouting, and the soot. The screams of soldiers burning alive. And the gold of the regiment's Aquila — untouched by soot or blood, the last unsullied piece of a world that was going mad."

“关于我的母亲和我从前的生活，那就是最后的记忆。那个时候，我还没有加入忠嗣学院，没有成为见习修女，没有通过考验，也没有许下誓言。”
"That was my last memory of my mother. And of my former life — before the Schola Progenium and the novitiate, before my trials, before the vows."

  • 选择 Choice

“你随身带着的那个金色碎片……”
"That golden shard you carry with you..."

“那是我自己的圣物，是那个军团的双头鹰徽章。或者换个说法，它是在袭击、爆炸与大火中幸存下来的碎片。对我来说，它仿佛是在提醒我——即便是在黑暗的核心，纯洁与光明也依然不会泯灭。”
"My own relic. It's the regiment's Aquila, or rather, the fragment that survived the attack, the explosions, and the fire. For me it's a reminder that purity and radiance can be preserved even in the heart of darkness."

  • 选择 Choice

“你是如何成为修女会的一员的？”
"So how did you become one of the Adepta Sororitas?"

“‘成为’……这个词很古怪。虽然听起来没问题，但这个词真的可以用来谈论命定之事吗？如果你问的是我选择的道路本身，那这个问题很容易回答。我像许多其他孤儿一样，在忠嗣学院熬了很多年。那段日子很难熬，但也是我美好的记忆，因为很少有什么能比得上通过试炼之后的满足感。即便试炼会让你的身体因疲惫而疼痛，让你的灵魂在痛苦中抽搐，也无所谓。”
"'Become'... It's such a strange word for it. It seems right, but is that how one talks about their destiny? If you're asking about the path itself — that's easy enough to answer. First, like many other orphans, I endured the Schola Progenium. Those years were rough, but I remember the hardship fondly. Few things can compare with the feeling of satisfaction from a passed trial, even if it leaves your body aching from exhaustion or your soul wincing in pain."

“我是同龄人中的佼佼者，被选为修女会的见习修女。当那重要的时刻到来时，我通过了考验，宣读了我的誓词。那是我人生中最快乐的一天！尽管帝皇的光明一直伴随着我，但全心全意地接受祂的光芒，许下那些誓言时——那简直是一种无与伦比的狂喜。”
"I was one of the best among my peers. And I was selected for the novitiate in the ranks of the Adepta Sororitas. When the hour came, I passed the trials and took my vows. The most joyous day of my life! The Emperor's light has always been with me, but to accept it with all your heart, to utter the oaths — that is a rapture like no other."

  • 选择 Choice

“你有没有期望过不同的命运？”
"Have you ever wished for a different lot in life?"

这个问题似乎让阿洁塔措手不及。“我有没有期望过……？可那会是可耻的弱点，几乎算是异端邪说！当然没有，我生来就是为了成为修女。我为帝皇的意志而生。在祂的明光中，我也成为了明光。我必须成为明光，这既是为了我自己，也是为了那些寻求我保护的人。”
The question seems to catch Argenta off guard. "Have I ever...? But that would be shameful weakness, almost heresy! Of course not. I was born for this. I live by the Emperor's will and in His light, I myself am the light, I must be the light — for myself and for those who ask for my protection."

“帝皇选择我来侍奉祂。但除此之外我并不否认——每当我一想到，那些被我射杀的异端分子再也无法让别的孩子沦为孤儿，我就会感到兴奋不已。”
"I was chosen to serve. But beyond that — I won't deny it — few things elate me as much as the thought that the heretic felled by my shot will never again orphan a child."

"Thank you for your candour."

阿洁塔低下了头。“能与你坦诚相待，这是……我的荣幸。”
Argenta bows her head. "It is... my pleasure to be candid."

  • 选择 Choice

“提醒我一下，咱们要干什么？”

"To find the way to the planet called Salis Prime. Saint Argenta is my patroness, and that is where her fallen ship is. And it must also be the resting place of her great relic — the One Star."

  • 选择 Choice

“和我说说圣阿洁塔的事情吧，就是你在寻找的那件圣物的主人。”
"Tell me about Saint Argenta, whose relic you're searching for."

“我很乐意！听好……”她半闭着眼睛，讲起了故事，声音几乎像是歌唱一样。“很久以前，有个受到祝福的世界。天空上照耀着成千上万颗星星。群星是如此璀璨，那里的居民几乎都不知道夜晚有多么黑暗。成千上万条河流滋养着土地。每到春天，成千上万座花园便会有鲜花绽放。每时每刻，都有成千上万的祈祷者在天空中飞翔。他们感谢着，赞美着帝皇。”
"Gladly! Listen..." She begins her tale, her eyes half-closed and her voice almost singing: "Long ago, there was a blessed world. Thousands of stars covered the sky there, so bright that its denizens hardly knew the darkness of night. Thousands of rivers nurtured the soil, thousands of gardens bloomed every spring, and at every moment, thousands of prayers were flying into the clear air, thanking and praising the Emperor."

“但突然有一天，人们明白了黑暗的含义。一大群该死的异端分子仿佛风暴一样降临到了这颗行星，他们将灵魂出卖给了混沌大敌。炮弹从天而降，城市被夷平，花园被烧毁，河里流满了虔诚之人的鲜血。硝烟与烟尘遮天蔽日，吞没了曾经照亮这个世界的群星。”
"But one day, the people learned the meaning of darkness. Like a storm, accursed heretics who had sold themselves to the Archenemy descended upon the planet. Shells flew from the sky that desolated whole cities, and burned the gardens, and filled the riverbeds with the blood of the faithful. Smoke and soot swallowed the skies and the thousand stars that had once shone over the world."

“在为数不多的幸存者中，有一个孤儿。她所有家人都死在了她面前，她从小到大长大的花园化为了灰烬。但在她心中，她恪守着绝对的真理，那就是——帝皇会保佑祂的人民。怀着这样的信念，她紧紧地盯着被烟尘覆盖的阴暗天空。可怕的天空中，明亮的星星全都销声匿迹了……只有一颗还在。”
"Among the handful of survivors was one orphan who had watched all her family die and the garden she'd grown up in burn to ash. But in her heart, she knew the absolute truth, just these three words — the Emperor protects. And knowing that, she never looked away from the black, terrifying, smoke-covered sky. There were no more bright stars to be seen... except for one."

“唯一一颗明亮的星星，命运之星，在天空中闪耀着。当那个孤儿对它露出微笑时，命运之星恰好落在了她的手中。那片大陆的所有虔诚之人，都看到了星星落入人间的那一幕。他们认为这是个预兆，前往星星落下的地方。他们团结起来，在命运之星的光芒下，找到了他们的救赎之路。”
"The One Star, the bright star, the silver star shone in the sky. And when the orphan smiled at it — the One Star fell right into her hands. All the faithful in every corner of the continent who saw the trail of the falling star recognised it as an omen and went looking for the place where it landed. And they rallied together, and with the light of the One Star, they found their salvation."

  • 选择 Choice

“这个故事里的女孩就是圣阿洁塔吗？”
"The girl from the story — that was Saint Argenta?"

“没错，那就是她传奇生涯的开端。众所周知，她生活的世界遭遇了动荡，那个世界的异端分子发动了一场可怕的叛乱。他们消灭了整颗行星上的所有生命——除了阿洁塔靠着命运之星与信仰的力量救下来的那些人。”
"Yes. That was the beginning of her hagiography. It is known that she lived on a world where heretics staged a terrible insurrection. They wiped out all life on the planet — except those whom Saint Argenta managed to save with the One Star. And with the strength of her faith."

“在那之后，她乘坐着带有银星印记的飞船，穿梭于无数动荡的世界中，给那些世界的虔诚之人带来了希望。许多官方记载都可以证实这样的说法。她的到来帮助当地的人们扭转了战局，让他们赶在帝国主力部队抵达之前就消灭了腐化的痕迹。”
"After that she travelled between worlds gripped by turmoil on her ship marked with a silver star and brought hope to the faithful. Numerous accounts confirm this. Her coming helped people turn the tide of the war and wipe away corruption before the Imperium's main forces even arrived."

“几百万人感谢她的救命之恩。然而，当那些异端分子意识到他们的阴谋即将破产时，他们派出了所有的残余部队，追杀那艘带着银星印记的飞船。那艘飞船从空中坠落，落到了某个不知名的世界。关于阿洁塔当时的年纪，并没有确切的记录。在一部分编年史中，她甚至被称为童子圣人，不过这些记录的可信度相当值得怀疑。总之，无论怎样，她并没有活得很久……但她就像落入人间的星星一样，留下了一道明亮的轨迹。”
"Millions of people owed their lives to her. But the heretics, having realised their imminent defeat, sent the remnants of their forces after the ship with the silver star. It fell from the skies onto an obscure world. There are no definitive records of how old Argenta was at the time. In some chronicles she's even called the Child Saint, but their credibility is questionable. Either way, she didn't live long... but she left a bright trail in her wake. Like a falling star."

  • 选择 Choice

“这个‘命运之星’究竟是什么东西？”
"So what is this One Star?"

“噢，要是我知道那是什么就好了！无论是圣传还是各种传说，都没有给出过明确的答案。古典圣像画师认为，这颗星星变成了一面用银丝织成的旗帜。当这面旗帜被带到战场上时，它会发出明亮的光芒，只会晃瞎异端分子的眼睛，不会伤害虔诚之人。 在绝大部分画师的笔下，圣阿洁塔的形象都是举着旗帜的姑娘。”
"Oh, if I only knew! Neither the hagiography nor the legends give a straight answer. Classical iconographers believed that the star turned into a banner woven from silver thread, which, when brought onto the battlefield, would shed light that blinded only heretics but did no harm to the faithful. Most of them portrayed Saint Argenta as a girl carrying this banner."

“还有人认为，命运之星从天上掉下来之后，变成了一把神圣的链锯剑。他们认为阿洁塔挥舞着那把链锯剑，击溃了怪物与帝国之敌。而在一部分早期雕刻作品中，阿洁塔的形象是穿着动力装甲的战士，胸前有一颗银色的星星。某种神学理论身为，这件动力装甲正是那件圣遗物。还有一部分人甚至认为，命运之星实际上指的是阿洁塔乘坐的那艘飞船。”
"Others think that upon falling from the sky, the One Star became a holy chainsword, which Argenta later used to strike down monsters and enemies of the Imperium. In some of the earlier engravings, Argenta is depicted wearing power armour with a silver star on her chest — one theological theory suggests that this armour was, in fact, the relic. Some even think that the One Star is actually the ship on which Argenta travelled."

她的双眼闪闪发光。“这个问题几千年来一直在困扰着国教。我认为，当我找到这个问题的答案时，就完成了我的使命！我祈祷我们能尽快找到通往萨利斯主星的航路……毁灭之力肯定会联合起来阻止我们，他们肯定会阻挡信仰的道路。”
Her eyes gleam. "I feel that my undertaking will be fulfilled when I find the answer that has eluded the Ecclesiarchy for millennia! I pray we find the way to Salis Prime soon... The Ruinous Powers must be aligned against us. They stand in the way of faith."

  • 选择 Choice

“我没有别的问题要问了。”
"I have no more questions."

“总有一天，我们会抵达萨利斯主星，站在圣阿洁塔飞船的大门之前……我知道，我确信。”
"One day we will reach Salis Prime and stand before the gates of Saint Argenta's ship... I know it. I believe."

"What is it that's keeping you in my retinue?"

"This ship was targeted by heretics — which means that my presence here and the assistance I provide to you are my sacred duty. Sooner or later I will likely have to return to Footfall, to protect its reliquary. But for now I wish to remain a part of the Rogue Trader's crew."

"It pleases me to have a servant of the Golden Throne in my crew. May the enemies of the Imperium tremble before our onslaught!"

阿洁塔的双眼闪着光。“敌人必将灭亡！”

“我想跟你讨论一下，你从欧夫拉茨二号星的战斗中了解到了什么事情？”

"Of course!" Argenta heaves an agitated sigh. "Do you remember the first days of the attack, when we captured one of the heretic commanders? “那个异端分子是昆拉德·维特威尔最亲密的党羽之一。他痛苦的呼号向我揭示了我长久以来一直想知道的事情——通往萨利斯主星的道路的标志，那个我朝思暮想的世界！终末黎明的异端分子尽其所能地想阻止我们，但他们失败了。”
"The heretic was one of Kunrad Voigtvir's closest henchmen. And he revealed — screaming through the pain — what I had wanted to know for so long: the markers of the route to Salis Prime, the world my heart calls to! The heretics of the Final Dawn tried all they could to stop us, but they failed."

“我此刻愿意追随你，但不能保证永远在你身边。每个角落都潜伏着或隐或现的邪恶，如此之多的腐化与卑劣！我多么渴望把它们连根拔起，一个不留！无论在何时何地，无论要付出怎样的代价。”阿洁塔的双眼闪烁着危险的烈焰。“你背负了太多琐碎的烦恼，行商浪人。而我的道路则是一条直线，只会势不可挡，通向唯一的终点。”
"Today I do. But I cannot promise to always be at your side. There is so much evil, hidden and overt, so much corruption and vileness lurking in every corner! I yearn to sweep all of it away, to eradicate it — wherever I find it, whenever I find it, no matter the cost." Argenta's eyes burn dangerously. "You are burdened with too many trivial cares, Rogue Trader. Whereas my road is a straight line that leads inexorably to a single goal."
